        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer177152247" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7646418610834894956">I like Richard Laymon. He’s a quick read which means that I can get the sense of accomplishment from reading a book and not feeling like a slug. I was trying to read The Alienist by Caleb Carr before reading this book and was having a hard time getting into it. Back to Endless Night, basic plot, girl, Jody is staying over a friends house when a bunch of crazies break in and kill almost everyone except her and her friends little brother. They escape and one of the crazies, Simon follows them. The</span>
  <span id="freeText7646418610834894956" style="display:none">I like Richard Laymon. He’s a quick read which means that I can get the sense of accomplishment from reading a book and not feeling like a slug. I was trying to read The Alienist by Caleb Carr before reading this book and was having a hard time getting into it. Back to Endless Night, basic plot, girl, Jody is staying over a friends house when a bunch of crazies break in and kill almost everyone except her and her friends little brother. They escape and one of the crazies, Simon follows them. The story is then told switching between Jody and Simon as they each move forward towards their inevitable confrontation. Like I said, it’s a fun ride and it full of the usual Laymon nastiness. Recommended if you like horror novels.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7646418610834894956" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1369232590" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1369232590" />
    <a title="Ekel Adolf" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44064349-ekel-adolf"><img alt="Ekel Adolf" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544633596p2/44064349.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1369232590?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ekel Adolf" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ekel Adolf" href="/user/show/44064349-ekel-adolf">Ekel Adolf</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369232590" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12171117594282040140"><i>Endless Night</i> is one of the best of Laymon's work, being especially mercyless and thrilling and also quite experimental in the way the story is narrated. Albeit, the most charming aspect is maybe the metafictional one, since the gang of killers in <i>Endless Night</i> calls themselves the Krulls, a name which they got from a horror novel not mentioned by title, but being nothing else than Laymon's masterpiece <i>The Woods Are Dark</i>.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nmVCVgXYG85D5dplxhL4aC8FaM2PBsY03INeYIp78JjvnizNFSo8xPtXiql/QVGpMramBoKlFB3kDo5jC6bTUw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VDVn06rYoI4jk1pjws2lmKhWtS0Vu+PQVK0jlR+GGvQlzglIuiqHhJshCq97ngxZteV75hgYMflsIPOWnls5Pw==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/83937.Richard_Laymon">About Richard Laymon</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/83937.Richard_Laymon"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1410040528p3/83937.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8566322236396678049">Richard Laymon was born in Chicago and grew up in California. He earned a BA in English Literature from Willamette University, Oregon and an MA from Loyola University, Los Angeles. He worked as a schoolteacher, a librarian, and a report writer for a law firm, and was the author of more than thirty acclaimed novels. <br/><br/>He also published more than sixty short stories in magazines such as <i>Ellery Queen, </i></span>
  <span id="freeText8566322236396678049" style="display:none">Richard Laymon was born in Chicago and grew up in California. He earned a BA in English Literature from Willamette University, Oregon and an MA from Loyola University, Los Angeles. He worked as a schoolteacher, a librarian, and a report writer for a law firm, and was the author of more than thirty acclaimed novels. <br /><br />He also published more than sixty short stories in magazines such as <i>Ellery Queen, Alfred Hitchcock,</i> and <i>Cavalier,</i> and in anthologies including <i>Modern Masters of Horror.</i><br /><br />He died from a massive heart attack on February 14, 2001 (Valentine's Day). <br /><br />Also published under the name Richard Kelly </span>
  <a data-text-id="8566322236396678049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

All the windows were shut because of the air conditioner, and it was so smoky in there you’d think we each had our own cigars. If you ask me, gunsmoke smells a lot better than cigar smoke. Love it. But I was afraid people driving by might worry if they saw all that smoke, so I put my window down to let it out.&rdquo;</span>
